${{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = spatial background metric
${{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = difference of spatial metric and spatial background metric
${{{ \gamma} _i} _j} = {{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} + {{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j}}$ = spatial metric

${{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial background metric derivative
${{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = difference of spatial metric derivative and spatial background metric derivative, hyperbolic state variable
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial metric derivative
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$

${{{ b} ^i} _j} = {{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}}$
${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}} = {{{ b} ^i} _j}$

connections:
${{{{ \Gamma} _i} _j} _k} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\left({{{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k} _{,j}}} - {{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,i}}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \Gamma} _i} _k} _j} + {{{{ \Gamma} _j} _k} _i}}$

${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{\frac{1}{2}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,m}}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _k} _{,j}}}\right)}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{{ d} _k} _m} _j} - {{{{ d} _m} _j} _k}}}\right)}}}$
using ${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$
${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _m} _j} - {{{{ \hat{d}} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _m} _j} - {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _m} _j} _k}}}\right)}}}$

metric inverse partial:
${{\left( {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}\right)} _{,k}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _m} _{,k}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ d} _k} _l} _m}}}}$
using ${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _m} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _m}}\right)}}}}$

$\alpha$ = lapse

lapse derivative:
${{ a} _i} = {{\left( \log\left( \alpha\right)\right)} _{,i}}$
${{ a} _i} = {{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,i}}}$
${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$

lapse evolution:
${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{{{ \alpha} _{,i}}} {{{ \beta} ^i}}} - {{{{\alpha}^{2}}} {{f}} {{\left({{{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}} - {{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}\right)}}}}$
using ${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _i}}}$
${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}}$

lapse partial evolution
${{ { \alpha} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}$
using ${{{ \alpha} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{ { \alpha} _{,k}} _{,t}}$ ; ${{ \alpha} _{,k}} = {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}}}$
${{{{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{ a} _k}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}}} = {{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}$
using on lhs only ${{ a} _k} = {{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,k}}}$
${{{{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{\frac{1}{\alpha}} {{ \alpha} _{,k}}}}} + {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}}} = {{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}$
subtracting ${{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{\frac{1}{\alpha}}}$ from both sides
${{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}} = {{{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}} - {{{{ \alpha} _{,t}}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{\frac{1}{\alpha}}}}}$

${{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ a} _k} _{,t}}}} = {{{\left( {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}} - {{{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{\frac{1}{\alpha}}} {{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{\left({{{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}}\right)}}}}}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{\left( {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}\right)} _{,k}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{{{\left( {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}}} + {{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}}\right)} _{,k}} + {{\left( {{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _k}}\right)} _{,m}}} - {\left({{{{{ a} _k}} {{{{ b} ^m} _m}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{{ a} _k} _{,m}}}}}\right)}} - {{\left( {{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{ a} _m}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ b} ^m} _k}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^m}} {{{{ a} _m} _{,k}}}}}$
expanding rhs derivative
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ f} _{,k}}}} + {{{{ a} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _i} _{,k}}}} - {{{f}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ f} _{,k}}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{{{ a} _k}} {{{{ \beta} ^m} _{,m}}}} - {{{{ a} _k}} {{{{ b} ^m} _m}}}} - {{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ \beta} ^m} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ b} ^m} _k}}}}$

metric evolution:
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{{{-2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}} + {{{ \beta} _i} _{,j}} + {{{ \beta} _j} _{,i}}} - {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} _k} _i} _j}}}}$

metric delta evolution
${{\left( {{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} + {{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j}\right)} _{,t}} = {{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^k} _j}} {{\left({{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _k} + {{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _k}}\right)}}} + {{{{{ b} ^k} _i}} {{\left({{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _k} + {{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _k}}\right)}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{2}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)}}}}}}$

metric partial delta evolution:
${{\frac{1}{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,t}} _{,k}}} = {{\left( {\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} - {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}}}}\right)}\right)} _{,k}}$
using ${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$ ; ${{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{\left( {\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} - {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}}}}\right)}\right)} _{,k}}$
TODO move the ${{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j$ and ${{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j$ values outside of the derivative
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{{{{\left( {\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} - {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}}}}\right)}\right)} _{,k}} + {{\left( {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)} _{,l}}} - {\left({{{{{{ b} ^l} _l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,l}}}}}\right)}} - {{\left( {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,l}}}}}$
expanding rhs derivative
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} - {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ \beta} ^l} _{,l}}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}} + {{{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,l}}}} - {{{2}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ \beta} ^l} _{,k}}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}}}\right)}}$
using ${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,l}}$
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} - {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _l}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ \beta} ^l} _{,l}}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}} + {{{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,l}}}} - {{{2}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ \beta} ^l} _{,k}}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}}}\right)}}$

Riemann curvature
${{{{{ R} ^i} _j} _k} _l} = {{{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _l} _{,k}} - {{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} _{,l}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _l}}}} - {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _l}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _k}}}}$

Ricci curvature
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{{{ R} ^k} _i} _k} _j}$
using ${{{{{ R} ^i} _j} _k} _l} = {{{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _l} _{,k}} - {{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} _{,l}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _l}}}} - {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _m} _l}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _j} _k}}}}$
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _j} _{,k}} - {{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _i} _k} _{,j}}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _m} _k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _i} _j}}}} - {{{{{{ \Gamma} ^k} _m} _j}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^m} _i} _k}}}}$
using ${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{{ d} _k} _m} _j} - {{{{ d} _m} _j} _k}}}\right)}}}$
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{{{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^m}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _i} _m} _j} + {{{{{ d} _j} _m} _i} - {{{{ d} _m} _i} _j}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}} - {{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^m}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _i} _m} _k} + {{{{{ d} _k} _m} _i} - {{{{ d} _m} _i} _k}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,j}}} + {{{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _m} _l} _k} + {{{{{ d} _k} _l} _m} - {{{{ d} _l} _m} _k}}}\right)}}}} {{{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _i} _n} _j} + {{{{{ d} _j} _n} _i} - {{{{ d} _n} _i} _j}}}\right)}}}}}} - {{{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _m} _l} _j} + {{{{{ d} _j} _l} _m} - {{{{ d} _l} _m} _j}}}\right)}}}} {{{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _i} _n} _k} + {{{{{ d} _k} _n} _i} - {{{{ d} _n} _i} _k}}}\right)}}}}}}$
cancel terms using symmetries:
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{{{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^m}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _i} _m} _j} + {{{{{ d} _j} _m} _i} - {{{{ d} _m} _i} _j}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}} - {{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^m}} {{{{{ d} _i} _m} _k}}\right)} _{,j}}} + {{{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _m} _l} _k}}}} {{{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _i} _n} _j} + {{{{{ d} _j} _n} _i} - {{{{ d} _n} _i} _j}}}\right)}}}}}} - {{{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _m} _l} _j} + {{{{{ d} _j} _l} _m} - {{{{ d} _l} _m} _j}}}\right)}}}} {{{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _i} _n} _k} + {{{{{ d} _k} _n} _i} - {{{{ d} _n} _i} _k}}}\right)}}}}}}$
split off terms to rearrange gradient:
${{{ R} _i} _j} = {{{{{{\left( {{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _l} _j}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _l} _i}}}} - {{{{ d} _l} _i} _j}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}} + {{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l} _{,k}}} {{\left({{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _i} _j} _l}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _j} _i} _l}}}}\right)}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^p}} {{{\left( {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _j}} {{{{ \delta} ^k} _i}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ d} _m} _p} _i}} {{{{ \delta} ^k} _j}}}\right)} _{,k}}}}} - {{\left( {{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{ \gamma} ^p} ^q}} {{\left({{{{{{{ d} _i} _p} _q}} {{{{ \delta} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{{ d} _j} _p} _q}} {{{{ \delta} ^k} _i}}}}\right)}}\right)} _{,k}}} + {{{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{{{{ d} _m} _l} _k}}}} {{{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _i} _n} _j} + {{{{{ d} _j} _n} _i} - {{{{ d} _n} _i} _j}}}\right)}}}}}} - {{{{{{{ \gamma} ^k} ^l}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _m} _l} _j} + {{{{{ d} _j} _l} _m} - {{{{ d} _l} _m} _j}}}\right)}}}} {{{{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{\left({{{{{ d} _i} _n} _k} + {{{{{ d} _k} _n} _i} - {{{{ d} _n} _i} _k}}}\right)}}}}}}$

combining derivatives

Gaussian curvature
${R} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{ R} _i} _j}}}$
using Ricci definition

as a system:
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{f}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{\frac{\partial f}{\partial \alpha}}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}}}}} + {{{{ a} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _k} _{,i}}}} - {{{f}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{\frac{\partial f}{\partial \alpha}}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}}}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _m}}} + {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{f}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _m}}} + {{{{{{ a} _k}} {{{{{{ \beta} ^m} _{,l}}} {{{{ \delta} ^l} _m}}}}} - {{{{ a} _k}} {{{{{{ b} ^m} _l}} {{{{ \delta} ^l} _m}}}}}} - {{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ \beta} ^m} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{ a} _m}} {{{{ b} ^m} _k}}}}$
